***statief.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:statief.html>statief</a> (29620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">statīvus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:statief.html>statief</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:statieven.html>statieven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:statief.html>statiefje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">tripod</span> serving as an optic <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> or other device's three-legged <span class="Latn" lang="en">stand</span> or <span class="Latn" lang="en">mount</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">drievoet</span> (wider)</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:driepoot.html>driepoot</a></span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:statief.html>statief</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:fotografie.html>fotografie</a>)</span>, <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(optica)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stabiel.html>stabiel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderstel.html>onderstel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:camera.html>camera</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kijker.html>kijker</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>ander</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:optisch.html>optisch</a>) instrument, <a href = vnd.unilang:veelal.html>veelal</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:draagbaar.html>draagbare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitvoering.html>uitvoering</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> één of <a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> inklapbare of inschuifbare <a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>Te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koop.html>koop</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> verrijdbaar <b><a href = vnd.unilang:statief.html>statief</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> studiogebruik.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:statisch.html>statisch</a> (33795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:statisch.html>statisch</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:statisch.html>statischer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:statisch.html>statisch</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">statischt</b>)
</p>

***statuut.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:statuut.html>statuut</a> (37724)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">statute</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">statut</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">statūtum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:statuut.html>statuut</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:statuten.html>statuten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:statuut.html>statuutje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>statute, legislation, regulation; written collection of laws or rules</li>
<li>statute; written rule or principle, especially of a society or other institution</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ordinance, law</li></ol>

***steden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:steden.html>steden</a> (3514)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:steden.html>steden</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">staden</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>. The verb derived from the sense of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a></i> meaning "place" in general, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now obsolete.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hold in place</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:steed.html>steed</a> (33014)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">steda</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stallion, stud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stoti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">herd of <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>horses</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">stuot</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">herd of <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>horses</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:steed.html>steed</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A stallion, especially in the sense of mount.
<dl><dd><i>The studded bridle on a ragged bough</i></dd>
<dd><i>Nimbly she fastens: <a href = vnd.unilang:--.html>--</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>, how quick <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> love! <a href = vnd.unilang:--.html>--</a></i></dd>
<dd><i>The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:steed.html>steed</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> stalled up, and <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> now</i></dd>
<dd><i>To tie the rider she begins to prove:</i></dd>
<dd><i>Backward she push'd him, as she would be thrust,</i></dd>
<dd><i>And govern'd him in strength, though not in <a href = vnd.unilang:lust.html>lust</a>.</i> — Shakespeare, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20140811201712/http://etext.virginia.edu/etcbin/ot2www-pubeng?specfile=%2Ftexts%2Fenglish%2Fmodeng%2Fpublicsearch%2Fmodengpub.o2w">"Venus and <a href = vnd.unilang:adonis.html>Adonis</a>".</a></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cycling<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> humorous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A bicycle.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stedes</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a></i>, an adverbial genitive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:steden.html>stede</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">steadfast, durable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with <a href = vnd.unilang:umlaut.html>umlaut</a> from the more common <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stade.html>stade</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stādi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stēdi-</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:steeg.html>steeg</a> (5237)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">steech</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stijgen.html>stege</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">steyga</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stega</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stairway</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stigǭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">staircase; <a href = vnd.unilang:ladder.html>ladder</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">stēge</i>, German <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:steg.html>Steg</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Shortening of older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">steentijdperk</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">steentijdvak</i>. Perhaps shortened after <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Steinzeit</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steen.html>steen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a></i>.

</p>
<ol><li>Stone Age <span class="defdate">[from 1860s]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">steentijdperk</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">steentijdvak</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stenen.html>stenen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijdperk.html>tijdperk</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:steiger.html>steiger</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">steger</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:steiger.html>steiger</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*staigriz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steiger.html>steiger</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steigers.html>steigers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steiger.html>steigertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a jetty; a small, often wooden landing for <a href = vnd.unilang:boats.html>boats</a> or small ships</li>
<li>scaffolding</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***stekelvarken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stekelvarken.html>stekelvarken</a> (26460)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1708, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stekel.html>stekel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spike</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:varken.html>varken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pig</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, perhaps through  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stachelschwein</i> (1556), eventually after the Romance family of <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> to which belong <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">porcospino</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">porcupine</i>. A slightly earlier Dutch word <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ijzervarken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">iron pig</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Afrikaans" class="extiw" title="w:Afrikaans"><a href = vnd.unilang:afrikaans.html>Afrikaans</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="af">ystervark</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stekelvarken.html>stekelvarken</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stekelvarkens.html>stekelvarkens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stekelvarken.html>stekelvarkentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A porcupine, large rodent of the <a href = vnd.unilang:families.html>families</a> Erethizontidae and Hystricidae.</li></ol>

***steken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:steken.html>steken</a> (1762)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stēken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stecan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stikaną</i>, originally a class 1 strong verb.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steken.html>steken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prick, sting</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stab, thrust (with a sharp instrument such as a dagger)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to insert, put in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoorde.html>hoorde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sleutel.html>sleutel</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slot.html>slot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gestoken.html>gestoken</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> a key being <b>inserted</b> into the keyhole.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***stell.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stell.html>stell</a> (50638)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:stellen.html>stellen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">stellan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to give a place to, set, place</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*stalljan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to put, position</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*stel-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to place, put, post, stand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stellen.html>stellen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to set, put</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:stellen.html>stellen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to put, place, fix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:stellen.html>stellen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to set, place, provide</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">steall</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">position, place</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">stall</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stell.html>stell</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">stells</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stelling.html>stelling</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">stelled</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">stold</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>  dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To place in position; set up, fix, plant; prop, mount.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To portray; delineate; display.
<ul><li><b>1594</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i>The Rape of Lucrece</i>, 1443–44:
<dl><dd>To this well-painted piece <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Lucrece come,</dd>
<dd>To find a face where all distress <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>stelled</b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1609</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, Sonnet 24:
<dl><dd>Mine eye hath play'd the painter and hath <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stell.html>stell</a>'d</b></dd>
<dd>Thy beauty's form in table of my heart ...</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Alteration of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stall</i>, after the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">to <a href = vnd.unilang:stell.html>stell</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stell.html>stell</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">stells</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A place; station.</li>
<li>A stall; a fold for cattle.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A prop; a support, as for the <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a> in standing or climbing.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A still.
<ul><li><b>1786</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Burns" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Robert Burns">Robert Burns</a>, "The Author's Earnest Cry And Prayer":
<dl><dd>Paint Scotland greetin owre her thrissle;</dd>
<dd>Her mutchkin stowp as <a href = vnd.unilang:toom.html>toom</a>'s a whissle;</dd>
<dd>An' damn'd excisemen in a bussle,</dd>
<dd>Seizin a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stell.html>stell</a></b>,</dd>
<dd>Triumphant crushin'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> like a mussel,</dd>
<dd>Or limpet shell!</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1791</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Burns" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Robert Burns">Robert Burns</a>, "Such a Parcel of Rogues in a Nation":
<dl><dd>The English <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stell.html>stell</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> could disdain,</dd>
<dd>Secure in valour's station;</dd>
<dd>But English gold <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> our bane-</dd>
<dd>Such a parcel of rogues in a nation!</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***stem.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> (896)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stemmen.html>stemme</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stemma</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stebnō</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stamnijō</i>. Under influence of Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:vox.html>vox</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">voice, word</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, it acquired the now obsolete sense of "word".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stemmen.html>stemmen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stemmetje.html>stemmetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>voice, sound made by the mouth using airflow</li>
<li>the ability to speak
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwijt.html>kwijt</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She’s <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> her <b>voice</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>vote</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> word</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">phonetics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> voice, property formed by vibration of the vocal cords</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_4">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a></strong>
</p>
